<li><a href="/wiki/Voiceverse_NFT_plagiarism_scandal" title="Voiceverse NFT plagiarism scandal">Voiceverse NFT plagiarism scandal</a></li></ul></div></div></td>
</tr><tr><td class="sidebar-content">
<div class="sidebar-list mw-collapsible mw-collapsed mw-made-collapsible"><button type="button" class="mw-collapsible-toggle mw-collapsible-toggle-default mw-collapsible-toggle-collapsed" aria-expanded="false" tabindex="0"><span class="mw-collapsible-text">show</span></button><div class="sidebar-list-title" style="border-top:1px solid #aaa; text-align:center;background-color:#e0e0e0;;color: var(--color-base)">Glossary</div><div class="sidebar-list-content mw-collapsible-content" hidden="until-found">

</tr><tr><td class="sidebar-navbar"><link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1333133064"><style data-mw-deduplicate="TemplateStyles:r1239400231">.mw-parser-output .navbar{display:inline;font-size:88%;font-weight:normal}.mw-parser-output .navbar-collapse{float:left;text-align:left}.mw-parser-output .navbar-boxtext{word-spacing:0}.mw-parser-output .navbar ul{display:inline-block;white-space:nowrap;line-height:inherit}.mw-parser-output .navbar-brackets::before{margin-right:-0.125em;content:"[ "}.mw-parser-output .navbar-brackets::after{margin-left:-0.125em;content:" ]"}.mw-parser-output .navbar li{word-spacing:-0.125em}.mw-parser-output .navbar a>span,.mw-parser-output .navbar a>abbr{text-decoration:inherit}.mw-parser-output .navbar-mini abbr{font-variant:small-caps;border-bottom:none;text-decoration:none;cursor:inherit}.mw-parser-output .navbar-ct-full{font-size:114%;margin:0 7em}.mw-parser-output .navbar-ct-mini{font-size:114%;margin:0 4em}html.skin-theme-clientpref-night .mw-parser-output .navbar li a abbr{color:var(--color-base)!important}@media(prefers-color-scheme:dark){html.skin-theme-clientpref-os .mw-parser-output .navbar li a abbr{color:var(--color-base)!important}}@media print{.mw-parser-output .navbar{display:none!important}}</style><div class="navbar plainlinks hlist navbar-mini"><ul><li class="nv-view"><a href="/wiki/Template:Artificial_intelligence" title="Template:Artificial intelligence"><abbr title="View this template">v</abbr></a></li><li class="nv-talk"><a href="/wiki/Template_talk:Artificial_intelligence" title="Template talk:Artificial intelligence"><abbr title="Discuss this template">t</abbr></a></li><li class="nv-edit"><a href="/wiki/Special:EditPage/Template:Artificial_intelligence" title="Special:EditPage/Template:Artificial intelligence"><abbr title="Edit this template">e</abbr></a></li></ul></div></td></tr></tbody></table>
<p><b>Mistral AI SAS</b> (<style data-mw-deduplicate="TemplateStyles:r1177148991">.mw-parser-output .IPA-label-small{font-size:85%}.mw-parser-output .references .IPA-label-small,.mw-parser-output .infobox .IPA-label-small,.mw-parser-output .navbox .IPA-label-small{font-size:100%}</style><span class="IPA-label IPA-label-small">French:</span> <span class="IPA nowrap" lang="fr-Latn-fonipa"><a href="/wiki/Help:IPA/French" title="Help:IPA/French">[mistal]</a></span>) is a French <a href="/wiki/Artificial_intelligence" title="Artificial intelligence">artificial intelligence</a> (AI) company, headquartered in <a href="/wiki/Paris" title="Paris">Paris</a>. Founded in 2023, it has open-weight <a href="/wiki/Large_language_model" title="Large language model">large language models</a> (LLMs), with both open-source and proprietary AI models.<sup id="cite_ref-:0_2-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:0-2"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>2<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-3"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>3<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-4"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>4<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup> As of 2025 the company has a valuation of more than US$14 billion.<sup id="cite_ref-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-5"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>5<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup>
</p>
<meta property="mw:PageProp/toc">
<div class="mw-heading mw-heading2"><h2 id="Namesake">Namesake</h2><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Mistral_AI&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: Namesake"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>
<p>The company is named after the <a href="/wiki/Mistral_(wind)" title="Mistral (wind)">mistral</a>, a powerful, cold wind in southern France,<sup id="cite_ref-Journal_6-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Journal-6"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>6<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup> a term which originates from the <a href="/wiki/Occitan_language" title="Occitan language">Occitan language</a>.
</p>
<div class="mw-heading mw-heading2"><h2 id="History">History</h2><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Mistral_AI&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: History"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>
<p>Mistral AI was established in April 2023 by three French AI researchers, <a href="/wiki/Arthur_Mensch" title="Arthur Mensch">Arthur Mensch</a>, Guillaume Lample and Timothe Lacroix.<sup id="cite_ref-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-7"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>7<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup>
</p><p>Mensch, an expert in advanced AI systems, is a former employee of <a href="/wiki/Google_DeepMind" title="Google DeepMind">Google DeepMind</a>; Lample and Lacroix, meanwhile, are large-scale AI models specialists who had worked for <a href="/wiki/Meta_Platforms" title="Meta Platforms">Meta Platforms</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-8"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>8<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup>
</p><p>The trio originally met during their studies at <a href="/wiki/%C3%89cole_polytechnique" title="cole polytechnique">cole Polytechnique</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Journal_6-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Journal-6"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>6<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup>
</p>
<figure typeof="mw:File/Thumb"><a href="/wiki/File:Mistral_AI_representation_(FLUX_Pro)_(cropped).webp" class="mw-file-description"><img src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/07/Mistral_AI_representation_%28FLUX_Pro%29_%28cropped%29.webp/330px-Mistral_AI_representation_%28FLUX_Pro%29_%28cropped%29.webp.png" decoding="async" width="265" height="269" class="mw-file-element" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/07/Mistral_AI_representation_%28FLUX_Pro%29_%28cropped%29.webp/500px-Mistral_AI_representation_%28FLUX_Pro%29_%28cropped%29.webp.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/07/Mistral_AI_representation_%28FLUX_Pro%29_%28cropped%29.webp/602px-Mistral_AI_representation_%28FLUX_Pro%29_%28cropped%29.webp.png 2x" data-file-width="602" data-file-height="611"></a><figcaption>Example of an image generated with <i>Le Chat</i>. The <a href="/wiki/Prompt_engineering" title="Prompt engineering">prompt</a> is: <code>Generate an image you feel represents yourself, Mistral AI.</code></figcaption></figure>
<figure typeof="mw:File/Thumb"><a href="/wiki/File:Le_Chat_chatbot_example_screenshot.webp" class="mw-file-description"><img src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/81/Le_Chat_chatbot_example_screenshot.webp/330px-Le_Chat_chatbot_example_screenshot.webp.png" decoding="async" width="265" height="186" class="mw-file-element" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/81/Le_Chat_chatbot_example_screenshot.webp/500px-Le_Chat_chatbot_example_screenshot.webp.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/81/Le_Chat_chatbot_example_screenshot.webp/612px-Le_Chat_chatbot_example_screenshot.webp.png 2x" data-file-width="612" data-file-height="429"></a><figcaption>Screenshot of <i>Le Chat</i>, Mistral AI chatbot, describing <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia" title="Wikipedia">Wikipedia</a> </figcaption></figure>
<div class="mw-heading mw-heading2"><h2 id="Company_operation">Company operation</h2><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Mistral_AI&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: Company operation"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>
<div class="mw-heading mw-heading3"><h3 id="Funding">Funding</h3><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Mistral_AI&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: Funding"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>
<p>In June 2023, the start-up carried out a first fundraising of 105 million ($117 million) with investors including the American fund <a href="/wiki/Lightspeed_Venture_Partners" title="Lightspeed Venture Partners">Lightspeed Venture Partners</a>, <a href="/wiki/Eric_Schmidt" title="Eric Schmidt">Eric Schmidt</a>, <a href="/wiki/Xavier_Niel" title="Xavier Niel">Xavier Niel</a> and <a href="/wiki/JCDecaux" title="JCDecaux">JCDecaux</a>. The valuation was then estimated by the <a href="/wiki/Financial_Times" title="Financial Times"><i>Financial Times</i></a> at 240 million ($267 million).
</p><p>On 10 December 2023, Mistral AI announced that it had raised 385 million ($428 million) as part of its second fundraising. This round of financing involves the Californian fund <a href="/wiki/Andreessen_Horowitz" title="Andreessen Horowitz">Andreessen Horowitz</a>, <a href="/wiki/BNP_Paribas" title="BNP Paribas">BNP Paribas</a> and the software publisher <a href="/wiki/Salesforce" title="Salesforce">Salesforce</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-9"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>9<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-10" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-10"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>10<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup>
</p><p>By December 2023, it was valued at over $2 billion.<sup id="cite_ref-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-11"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>11<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup>
</p><p>On 16 April 2024, reporting revealed that Mistral was in talks to raise 500 million, a deal that would more than double its current valuation to at least 5 billion.<sup id="cite_ref-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-12"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>12<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup>
</p><p>In June 2024, Mistral AI secured a 600 million ($645 million) funding round, increasing its valuation to 5.8 billion ($6.2 billion).<sup id="cite_ref-13" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-13"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>13<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup> Based on <a href="/wiki/Business_valuation" title="Business valuation">valuation</a>, as of June 2024, the company was ranked fourth globally in the AI industry, and first outside the <a href="/wiki/San_Francisco_Bay_Area" title="San Francisco Bay Area">San Francisco Bay Area</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-14" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-14"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>14<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup>
</p><p>In August 2025, the <i>Financial Times</i> reported that Mistral was in talks to raise $1 billion at a $10 billion valuation.<sup id="cite_ref-15" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-15"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>15<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup> In September 2025, <i>Bloomberg</i> announced that Mistral AI has secured a 2 billion investment valuing it at 12 billion ($14 billion).<sup id="cite_ref-16" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-16"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>16<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup> This comes after $1.5 billion investment from Dutch company <a href="/wiki/ASML_Holding" title="ASML Holding">ASML</a>, which owns 11% of Mistral.<sup id="cite_ref-17" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-17"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>17<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup>
</p>
<div class="mw-heading mw-heading3"><h3 id="Partnerships">Partnerships</h3><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Mistral_AI&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit section: Partnerships"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>
<p>On 26 February 2024, <a href="/wiki/Microsoft" title="Microsoft">Microsoft</a> announced that Mistral's language models would be made available on <a href="/wiki/Microsoft_Azure" title="Microsoft Azure">Microsoft's Azure cloud</a>, while the multilingual conversational assistant <i>Le Chat</i> would be launched in the style of <a href="/wiki/ChatGPT" title="ChatGPT">ChatGPT</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-18" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-18"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>18<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup><sup class="noprint Inline-Template noprint Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">[<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:No_original_research#Primary,_secondary_and_tertiary_sources" title="Wikipedia:No original research"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable secondary sources. (July 2025)">non-primary source needed</span></a></i>]</sup> The partnership also included a financial investment of $16 million by Microsoft in Mistral AI.<sup id="cite_ref-19" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-19"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>19<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup>
</p><p>In April 2025, Mistral AI announced a 100 million partnership with the shipping company <a href="/wiki/CMA_CGM" title="CMA CGM">CMA CGM</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-20" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-20"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>20<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-21" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-21"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>21<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup>
</p>
<div class="mw-heading mw-heading2"><h2 id="Services">Services</h2><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Mistral_AI&amp;action=edit&amp;section=6" title="Edit section: Services"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>
<p>On 19 November, 2024, the company announced updates for <i>Le Chat</i> (pronounced <span class="IPA nowrap" lang="fr-Latn-fonipa" title="Representation in the International Phonetic Alphabet (IPA)">/l<span class="wrap"> </span>a/</span> in <a href="/wiki/French_language" title="French language">French</a>, like the French word for "cat"). It added the ability to create images, using Black Forest Labs' <a href="/wiki/Flux_Pro" class="mw-redirect" title="Flux Pro">Flux Pro</a> model.<sup id="cite_ref-VentureBeat-LeChat_22-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-VentureBeat-LeChat-22"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>22<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup>
</p><p>On 6 February 2025, Mistral AI released <i>Le Chat</i> on <a href="/wiki/IOS" title="IOS">iOS</a> and <a href="/wiki/Android_(operating_system)" title="Android (operating system)">Android</a> mobile devices.<sup id="cite_ref-23" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-23"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>23<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup>
</p><p>Mistral AI also introduced a Pro subscription tier, priced at $14.99 per month, which provides access to more advanced models, unlimited messaging, and web browsing.<sup id="cite_ref-24" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-24"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>24<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup>
</p>
<div class="mw-heading mw-heading2"><h2 id="Models">Models</h2><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Mistral_AI&amp;action=edit&amp;section=7" title="Edit section: Models"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>

</p>

<td style="background: var(--background-color-interactive, #EEE); color: var(--color-base, black); vertical-align: middle; text-align: center;" class="table-Unknown">?
</td>
<td style="background: #E7E7FF; color:black; vertical-align: middle; text-align: center;" class="table-proprietary"><a href="/wiki/Proprietary_software" title="Proprietary software">Proprietary</a>
</td>
<td>Like the Large model, Mistral Small was launched on February 26, 2024.<sup id="cite_ref-Mistral_models_overview_40-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Mistral_models_overview-40"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>40<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<td>Mistral Large <i>24.02</i>
</td>
<td><span data-sort-value="000000002024-02-01-0000" style="white-space:nowrap">February 2024</span>
</td>
<td style="background: var(--background-color-interactive, #EEE); color: var(--color-base, black); vertical-align: middle; text-align: center;" class="table-Unknown">?
</td>
<td style="background: var(--background-color-interactive, #EEE); color: var(--color-base, black); vertical-align: middle; text-align: center;" class="table-Unknown">?
</td>
<td style="background: #E7E7FF; color:black; vertical-align: middle; text-align: center;" class="table-proprietary"><a href="/wiki/Proprietary_software" title="Proprietary software">Proprietary</a>
</td>
<td>Mistral Large was launched on February 26, 2024. It outputs in English, French, Spanish, German, and Italian, and provides coding capabilities.<sup id="cite_ref-52" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-52"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>52<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup> It is available on Microsoft Azure.<sup id="cite_ref-53" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-53"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>53<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Mistral_models_overview_40-13" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Mistral_models_overview-40"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>40<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<td>Mistral Medium
</td>
<td><span data-sort-value="000000002023-12-01-0000" style="white-space:nowrap">December 2023</span>
</td>
<td style="background: var(--background-color-interactive, #EEE); color: var(--color-base, black); vertical-align: middle; text-align: center;" class="table-Unknown">?
</td>
<td style="background: var(--background-color-interactive, #EEE); color: var(--color-base, black); vertical-align: middle; text-align: center;" class="table-Unknown">?
</td>
<td style="background: #E7E7FF; color:black; vertical-align: middle; text-align: center;" class="table-proprietary"><a href="/wiki/Proprietary_software" title="Proprietary software">Proprietary</a>
</td>
<td>Mistral Medium is trained in various languages including English, French, Italian, German, Spanish.<sup id="cite_ref-54" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-54"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>54<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup> The number of parameters, and architecture of Mistral Medium is not known as Mistral has not published public information about it.<sup id="cite_ref-Mistral_models_overview_40-14" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Mistral_models_overview-40"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>40<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<td>Mixtral 8x7B
</td>
<td><span data-sort-value="000000002023-12-01-0000" style="white-space:nowrap">December 2023</span>
</td>
<td style="background: var(--background-color-interactive, #EEE); color: var(--color-base, black); vertical-align: middle; text-align: center;" class="table-Unknown">?
</td>
<td>46.7
</td>
<td style="background: #9EFF9E; color:black; vertical-align: middle; text-align: center;" class="active table-active"><a href="/wiki/Apache_License" title="Apache License">Apache-2.0</a>
</td>
<td>Much like Mistral's first model, Mixtral 8x7B was released via a BitTorrent link posted on <a href="/wiki/Twitter" title="Twitter">Twitter</a> on December 9, 2023,<sup id="cite_ref-:0_2-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:0-2"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>2<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup> and later Hugging Face and a blog post were released two days later.<sup id="cite_ref-:1_55-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:1-55"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>55<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup> Unlike the previous Mistral model, Mixtral 8x7B uses a sparse <a href="/wiki/Mixture_of_experts" title="Mixture of experts">mixture of experts</a> architecture. The model has 8 distinct groups of "experts", giving the model a total of 46.7B usable parameters.<sup id="cite_ref-56" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-56"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>56<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-57" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-57"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>57<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup> Each single token can only use 12.9B parameters, therefore giving the speed and cost that a 12.9B parameter model would incur.<sup id="cite_ref-:1_55-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:1-55"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>55<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup> A version trained to follow instructions called Mixtral 8x7B Instruct is also offered.<sup id="cite_ref-:1_55-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:1-55"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>55<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Mistral_models_overview_40-15" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Mistral_models_overview-40"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>40<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<td>Mistral 7B
</td>
<td><span data-sort-value="000000002023-09-01-0000" style="white-space:nowrap">September 2023</span>
</td>
<td style="background: var(--background-color-interactive, #EEE); color: var(--color-base, black); vertical-align: middle; text-align: center;" class="table-Unknown">?
</td>
<td>7.3
</td>
<td style="background: #9EFF9E; color:black; vertical-align: middle; text-align: center;" class="active table-active"><a href="/wiki/Apache_License" title="Apache License">Apache-2.0</a>
</td>
<td>Mistral 7B is a 7.3B parameter language model using the transformers architecture. It was officially released on September 27, 2023, via a <a href="/wiki/BitTorrent" title="BitTorrent">BitTorrent</a> magnet link,<sup id="cite_ref-58" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-58"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>58<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup> and <a href="/wiki/HuggingFace" class="mw-redirect" title="HuggingFace">Hugging Face</a><sup id="cite_ref-59" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-59"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>59<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup> under the <a href="/wiki/Apache_2.0" class="mw-redirect" title="Apache 2.0">Apache 2.0</a> license. Both a base model and "instruct" model were released with the latter receiving additional tuning to follow chat-style prompts. The fine-tuned model is only intended for demonstration purposes, and does not have guardrails or moderation built-in.<sup id="cite_ref-:2_60-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:2-60"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>60<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Mistral_models_overview_40-16" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Mistral_models_overview-40"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>40<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup>
</td></tr></tbody><tfoot></tfoot></table>
<div class="mw-heading mw-heading3"><h3 id="Mistral_7B">Mistral 7B</h3><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Mistral_AI&amp;action=edit&amp;section=8" title="Edit section: Mistral 7B"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>
<p>Mistral AI claimed in the Mistral 7B release blog post that the model outperforms <a href="/wiki/LLaMA#LLaMA-2" class="mw-redirect" title="LLaMA">LLaMA 2</a> 13B on all benchmarks tested, and is on par with LLaMA 34B on many benchmarks tested,<sup id="cite_ref-:2_60-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:2-60"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>60<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup> despite having only 7 billion parameters, a small size compared to its competitors.
</p>
<div class="mw-heading mw-heading3"><h3 id="Mixtral_8x7B">Mixtral 8x7B</h3><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Mistral_AI&amp;action=edit&amp;section=9" title="Edit section: Mixtral 8x7B"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>
<p>Mistral AI claimed in 2023 that its model beat both LLaMA 70B, and <a href="/wiki/GPT-3" title="GPT-3">GPT-3.5</a> in most <a href="/wiki/Language_model#Evaluation_and_benchmarks" title="Language model">benchmarks</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-61" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-61"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>61<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup>
</p><p>In March 2024, research conducted by Patronus AI comparing performance of LLMs on a 100-question test with prompts to generate text from books protected under <a href="/wiki/Copyright_law_in_the_United_States" class="mw-redirect" title="Copyright law in the United States">U.S. copyright law</a> found that <a href="/wiki/OpenAI" title="OpenAI">OpenAI</a>'s <a href="/wiki/GPT-4" title="GPT-4">GPT-4</a>, Mixtral, <a href="/wiki/Meta_AI" title="Meta AI">Meta AI</a>'s <a href="/wiki/LLaMA#LLaMA-2" class="mw-redirect" title="LLaMA">LLaMA-2</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Anthropic" title="Anthropic">Anthropic</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Claude_(language_model)#Claude_2" title="Claude (language model)">Claude 2</a> generated copyrighted text verbatim in 44%, 22%, 10%, and 8% of responses respectively.<sup id="cite_ref-62" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-62"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>62<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-63" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-63"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>63<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup>
</p>
<div class="mw-heading mw-heading3"><h3 id="Mistral_Small_3.1">Mistral Small 3.1</h3><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Mistral_AI&amp;action=edit&amp;section=10" title="Edit section: Mistral Small 3.1"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>
<p>On 17 March 2025, Mistral released Mistral Small 3.1 as a smaller, more efficient model.<sup id="cite_ref-64" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-64"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>64<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup><sup class="noprint Inline-Template noprint Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">[<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:No_original_research#Primary,_secondary_and_tertiary_sources" title="Wikipedia:No original research"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable secondary sources. (May 2025)">non-primary source needed</span></a></i>]</sup><sup id="cite_ref-65" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-65"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>65<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup>
</p>
<div class="mw-heading mw-heading3"><h3 id="Mistral_Medium_3">Mistral Medium 3</h3><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Mistral_AI&amp;action=edit&amp;section=11" title="Edit section: Mistral Medium 3"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>
<p>On 7 May 2025, Mistral AI released Mistral Medium 3.<sup id="cite_ref-66" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-66"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>66<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup><sup class="noprint Inline-Template noprint Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">[<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:No_original_research#Primary,_secondary_and_tertiary_sources" title="Wikipedia:No original research"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable secondary sources. (May 2025)">non-primary source needed</span></a></i>]</sup>
</p>
<div class="mw-heading mw-heading3"><h3 id="Magistral_Small_and_Magistral_Medium">Magistral Small and Magistral Medium</h3><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Mistral_AI&amp;action=edit&amp;section=12" title="Edit section: Magistral Small and Magistral Medium"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>
<p>On 10 June 2025, Mistral AI released their first AI reasoning models: Magistral Small (open-source), and Magistral Medium, models which are purported to have <a href="/wiki/Prompt_engineering#Chain-of-thought" title="Prompt engineering">chain-of-thought</a> capabilities.<sup id="cite_ref-67" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-67"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>67<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-68" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-68"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>68<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup>
</p>
<div class="mw-heading mw-heading3"><h3 id="Mistral_Large_3_and_Ministral_3">Mistral Large 3 and Ministral 3</h3><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Mistral_AI&amp;action=edit&amp;section=13" title="Edit section: Mistral Large 3 and Ministral 3"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>
<p>On 2 December 2025, Mistral AI released Mistral Large 3, a sparse, mixture-of-experts model with 41 billion active parameters and 675 billion total parameters, and Ministral 3, three small, dense models with 3 billion, 7 billion and 14 billion parameters. <sup id="cite_ref-mistral3_29-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-mistral3-29"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>29<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup>
</p>
<div class="mw-heading mw-heading3"><h3 id="Devstral_2_and_Devstral_Small_2">Devstral 2 and Devstral Small 2</h3><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Mistral_AI&amp;action=edit&amp;section=14" title="Edit section: Devstral 2 and Devstral Small 2"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>
<p>On  10 December 2025, Mistral AI released Devstral 2 and Devstral Small 2. Devstral Small 2, a 24B parameter model is claimed to achieve better performance at coding than  Qwen 3 Coder Flash model which is a 30B parameter model.<sup id="cite_ref-69" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-69"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>69<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup>
</p>
<div class="mw-heading mw-heading2"><h2 id="Mistral_Vibe">Mistral Vibe</h2><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Mistral_AI&amp;action=edit&amp;section=15" title="Edit section: Mistral Vibe"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>
<p>On  10 December 2025, Mistral released Mistral Vibe, a <a href="/wiki/Command_line_interface" class="mw-redirect" title="Command line interface">command line interface</a> for AI-Assisted software development. This was initially released with the Devstral 2 and Devstral Small 2 models available.
</p>
